Description_12	In addition to blocking incoming ARMS, Twintelle's aura has a beguiling fragrance,\nwith top notes of jasmine and rose atop a base of knock-you-out.

Description_21	When wearing her fighting suit, Mechanica has to be careful that\nthe suit doesn't overheat...and that she doesn't overheat either!
Description_22	Check out Misango wearing a suit from Twintelle's fashion line.\nMy bow tie is also from her collection—I love her stuff!
Description_23	It's hard to play it cool when you've got flashing red lights on your heads...

Description_36	It's hard to sell my famous ARMS cookies when competing with Lola Pop...

Description_38	Apparently Misango starts each day at the Temple Grounds with this impressive workout!\nI hear he's also responsible for repairing those pillars whenever they're damaged...
Description_39	Mechanica is as brilliant an engineer as she is a fighter!\nThe ARMS League often hires her to help with advanced repairs.

Description_41	Hedlok got you in a headlock? Sounds rough, but Mechanica takes care\nof her customers in order of arrival—so keep it down, would ya!

Description_49	Check out Min Min and Master Mummy all dressed up for Halloween!\nWell, I guess Master Mummy is always ready for trick-or-treating...
Description_50	In Japan, playing with spinning tops is a traditional way to celebrate the New Year.\nLooks like Kid Cobra and Ninjara found a way to put their own, er, spin on this!
Description_51	What a day! Waving that huge banner was a lot harder than it looked.
Description_52	Check out these fighters in their street clothes helping\npromote ARMS badges. I gotta say, this is a stylish bunch!
Description_53	This was the thank-you note we made for those who checked out ARMS at a special event!
Description_54	That tower in the background sure looks familiar...
Description_55	Here's a neat image of all the original ARMS fighters together.\nWe made this to thank everyone for supporting our crazy new sport!
Description_56	The earliest materials we have relating to the ARMS ability date from 1,500 years ago. However,\nsome experts believe it has existed for at least 4,000 years. The hallmark "coiling like a spring"\nphenomenon can be found not just in people but in animals and plant life as well.
Description_57	The number of people with the ARMS ability is rapidly increasing; currently 20 percent of the population is affected.\nConsidering that some of those affected may not yet have reported to the ARMS League, it may even be higher than that.\nThough once deemed an oddity, in this day and age the ability is considered a gift and those with it are strongly admired.
Description_58	The arms of those with the ARMS ability transform into either "something deeply connected to the individual"\nor "something that was nearby at the time of their 'awakening.'" Or at least this is the current theory.\nHowever, there are some known examples of cases that do not follow this pattern...\nAn investigator is currently shadowing one of these outliers—report to follow.
Description_59	As previously stated, the ARMS ability is nothing new, but ARMS as a sport only dates back about 120 years.\nOne particular attribute of the ability's nature had previously prevented competition, but that all changed\nthanks to the special masks invented by the ARMS Ministry (what we call ARMS Labs today).
Description_60	The ARMS ability often emerges overnight, with those affected discovering their transformation upon waking up.\nAwakenings are most common during the teenage years, though in some individuals the ability has lain dormant\nfor as many as 74 years. Some are even born with the ability, though this is extremely rare.
Description_61	Based on our current research, only 1 in 100,000 individuals is born with the ARMS ability already manifest.\nIn the current league, Kid Cobra is the only example of this. He never removes his mask and has never disclosed\nanything about his family. He presents an extremely rare and interesting subject—investigation of him must be prioritized.
Description_62	The issue of arms unraveling and changing shape without regard to their subject's will was solved by\nthe invention of special masks, which allowed for sparring via extendable arms. As a result, formalized\ncompetitions quickly gained momentum. In the present day, these masks are provided to those with the\nARMS ability free of charge, manufactured by ARMS Labs and distributed by the ARMS League.
Description_63	The irises of those with the ARMS ability take on a spiral shape. This led to the hypothesis that the ability\ncould be controlled indirectly via the eyes, leading to the development of special masks. In order to prevent\ntheir misuse, the underlying technology is a closely guarded secret, only disclosed at the discretion of "Doctor C."
Description_64	The ARMS Ministry named the new sport that was created around the unique extendable-arm ability simply "ARMS."\nWhen the sport gained enough attention to sustain a professional league, the ministry changed its name and split\ninto two organizations. Tournament organization and fighter development would become the job of the ARMS League,\nand foundational research on the ARMS ability and the development of related products became the focus of ARMS Labs.
Description_65	There are no other known cases of the ARMS ability appearing in hair. Subject has refused requests for examination\nthree times so far. We sent a few staff members to infiltrate and hopefully return with some stray hairs, but we've lost\ncommunication with all of them. Perhaps she doesn't even have the true ARMS ability? But then how do you explain her eyes...
Description_66	The weapons used in ARMS (also called ARMS) were initially basic boxing-type gloves in the early days of the sport.\nIn the modern era, however, a wide range of different ARMS with unique characteristics is available to competitors.\nThe contributions of private corporations had a lot to do with this increased variety, but it's also well-known that\nwithout the technical support of ARMS Labs, there would be nowhere near the variety of ARMS currently available.
Description_67	Recently some fighters who do not possess the true ARMS ability have emerged in the professional ranks.\nColloquially these competitors are referred to as the "second generation." Mechanica and the test subject\nHelix are among them. Their rise has had a massive impact on the sport, inspiring even more interest from fans.
Description_68	Even among "second generation" fighters, Byte & Barq are unique. They showed up to their pre-Grand Prix\ninspection in their combined form... Having passed that, we were unable to stop them from participating,\neven after the truth of their partnership was revealed. It may be time to reevaluate how we conduct those\ninspections. That said, the commish is a big fan of theirs, so perhaps nothing will change.
Description_69	Doctor C refuses to fully reveal themself to us, so we've done some research in secret.\nThey're a once-in-a-generation genius, the youngest in history to rise to the top of ARMS Labs.\nUnconfirmed rumors abound, such as possessing 52 doctorates...and lacking the ability to taste food...
Description_70	The special masks used by ARMS fighters allow them to maintain their arms in a coiled state.\nIf the masks are removed, their arms become nearly impossible to control, coiling and uncoiling at random.\nIf you discover you have the ARMS ability, please contact the ARMS League outreach center by phone immediately!
Description_71	"Project Wearable Weapon," intended for use as a sparring partner for fighters, has been initiated. In essence,\nwe created the ultimate sandbag. Doctor C is the project lead. This is my first time working with them, so I'm\nquite excited. Will the average fighter be able to control so many arms at once? This will be our initial challenge.
Description_72	We're no closer to overcoming our initial challenge. A method of forcibly boosting brain power was proposed,\nbut Doctor C dismissed it. We've begun tests based on their idea of "expanding the thought capabilities of the device."\nWe've also modified the device from being worn on the torso to instead being placed atop the head. The doctor\nresponds to our communications promptly but refuses to appear before us. It's a bit unnerving...
Description_73	The prototype has escaped. Now able to "think," Hedlok has disappeared and seems in search of something.\nThis is an emergency. However, the doctor's interests have already moved elsewhere. We've been instructed\nto create a version that can be more easily equipped and unequipped. We'll leave the escaped Hedlok\nfor the fighters to deal with. In the end, I suppose it will have become a sparring partner for them...
Description_74	A long-sought victory finally realized. I was almost as happy as he was!
Description_75	What better way to celebrate with your fans than with a concert!\nI know people who know people and scored a front-row seat.
Description_76	What a magnificent display of ninjutsu! You know, I've been thinking about enrolling at Ninja College...
Description_77	What a miraculous reunion with his family thanks to them seeing Master Mummy on TV!\nIt was super emotional—thankfully they had plenty of gauze to dry their eyes.
Description_78	Min Min's victory brought tons of new customers and rave reviews to her family's Mintendo Noodle House. *slurp*
Description_79	After her victory, everyone wanted to know more about Mechanica's fighting suit!\nFrankly, her lecture about it was a bit (OK, like, a million miles) over my head...
Description_80	Victory made Twintelle's movies even more popular than before.\nThe rise of her star knows no limits—she's a supernova!
Description_81	Winning the Grand Prix earned Byte & Barq a much-needed vacation.\nLounge chairs and fruity drinks? That's my kinda beach patrol!
Description_82	Victory has elevated Kid Cobra's popularity into the stratosphere.\nGetting a selfie with him is the ultimate bragging right—even for me!
Description_83	After his big win, Helix returned to the empty lab... But don't worry—I'm looking after him!
Description_84	The commish adds yet another championship belt to his collection!
Description_85	Lola Pop used her Grand Prix prize money to open the circus of her dreams!\nShe even hired me to help spread the word.
Description_86	Misango invited me along for his celebratory trip back to his homeland.\nAnd man, the Misangans were sure happy to see me for some reason!
Description_87	After Springtron's victory, a lone child approached him before anyone noticed... My heart was in my throat!
Description_88	Uh, th-this is... Sorry, no comment! Memories are a precious thing...
Description_89	What an extravagant victory banquet! The winner of the ARMS Grand Prix is...you of course!

Reference_USen_szs\Reference_WeaponGuide.msbt
Normal	Packing a fiery punch with a good balance of\noffense and defense, you can't call yourself\na real fighter until you master these bad boys.
Thunder	Crank up your game—these gloves are electric!\nGreat for shocking and stunning opponents,\nthese and Toasters are the most popular ARMS.
Beginner	Solid all-around gloves that buff up in size.\nOriginally designed for beginners, they've\nbecome a favorite of many high-level fighters.
NormalPro	High-risk, high-reward explosive gloves that\ndetonate on impact. They lack a guidance\nsystem, so they'll really test your skills.
Revolver	These babies fire off three electrified shots,\none after another. Keep your opponents on\ntheir toes—only one has to hit to shock 'em!
ShotgunA	Featuring a wide attack range, these are good\nfor quick strikes and slowing opponents down.\nHighly recommended if you have bad aim.
Tornado	While they may look fun, getting caught\nin their dizzying spin is anything but a party.\nThey're great for surprising opponents, though!
Boomerang	Thanks to their looping flight path, obstacles\nain't no thing. Charge 'em up to unleash\na cyclone that'll send your opponent flying!
Chakram	Their quick, curving attack leaves no escape!\nOnce an ancient ninja weapon, modern\ntechnology has revitalized their appeal.
Bird	These wild birds dart up, down, left, and right\nas they please. And when they catch fire,\nthey look about as cool as anything ever.
Whip	Sweeping across a wide attack radius in a\nserpentine motion, these wily weapons will\nmake short work of any wannabe sidesteppers.
Parasol	When it's raining fists, grab one of these!\nThe undeniable elegance of these umbrellas\nwill leave your opponent's head spinning.
Homing	Not big on aiming? These auto-targeting ARMS\nare for you! They fly and explode all on their own.\nWhy mess around with controls? Delegate!
Big	The holy trinity of powerful ARMS: big, heavy,\nand slow. Not just capable weapons, these\nreliable lugs make sturdy shields as well!
Phalanx	These shield ARMS are steadily advancing\nstalwarts that can support a wide range of\nboth offensive and defensive fighting styles!
Laser	These 4,000-year-old grilling machines spread\nheat over a wide area. So when you fire 'em up,\ntake your time and cook your foes thoroughly.
Vertical	These jump-busting ARMS fire out three shots\nin a vertical stack. They're great for keeping\nballistic heat on any hop-happy opponents.
Bound	Big, bouncy, bulbous blobs of unknown origin.\nThe latest research suggests that they're very\nsticky and have a fantastic fruit-like flavor.
HammerWhip	These bulky ARMS shrug off attacks and give\ngreat peace of mind! Originally developed for\nconstruction, they're now refined for competition.
Ice	These sub-zero gloves are as cool as it gets.\nGreat for putting opponents on ice, they're\nalso nice for keeping postmatch drinks cold.
Inferno	Blue flames give these gloves maximum hotness.\nNo guidance system means higher damage output,\nmaking them a favorite of high-level fighters.
BigCp	Big! Strong! Heavy! High-powered! Electrified!\nWhat more do you want?! They're a bit slower\nthan Megatons but pack just as much punch.
HomingCp	Designed to hunt down and shock bad guys,\nthese were originally developed as crime stoppers!\nThe farther away an opponent, the better they do.
ShotgunCp	Blasting out three simultaneous shots\nin horizontal formation, their wide blast\nradius leaves little room for escape!
TornadoCp	Their generous spread attack feels like a party!\nShooting out stars in a spiral configuration,\nthey just scream "Congrats! Now BURN."
RevolverCp	Someone put some Revolvers together wrong,\nand now they shoot fire! Happy accidents are\nthe best accidents—until they catch you on fire.
BoomerangCp	Perfect for capturing prey and flash-freezing\nit to seal in that ultimate freshness. They\nalso work great as fans in the summertime.
BirdCp	A bird in the hand is worth two in an opponent's\nface, especially if they're electrically charged\nand ready to attack from any direction!
WhipCp	Extending across the battlefield like sharply\ncurving whips, these ARMS snake, expand,\nand send opponents flying when they connect.
LaserCp	These 4,000-year-old cooling machines take a bit\nto warm up, but they'll freeze opponents in their\ntracks quicker than snow on a school day.
ChakramCp	That same curving path you know and love,\nnow with fire! Great for charring opponents\nquick and thoroughly—or for cooking dinner!
BeginnerCp	Great all-around gloves that buff up big. Designed\nas an entry point for curving ARMS, many fighters\nnow appreciate their straightforward abilities.
HammerWhipCp	Smash and explode all in one power combo!\nOriginally designed for demolishing buildings,\ntheir destructive power is second to none.
Nunchuck	Its whirling stick thwacks opponents silly and will\nswitch up its spin during jumps. You may feel the\nneed to yell "hi-yah" while it's equipped.
Reflector	It's finally here—a shield that repels ARMS!\nAny attack that hits this puppy ricochets back\nat an opponent. How'd we ever live without it?
VerticalCp	Stamps a certain beloved commentator's image\nonto your opponent's face and marks particularly\njumpy foes. Not a valid passport stamp.
Scorpion	A scorpion that scuttles, jumps on opponents,\nand poisons them! Watch it curl up into a little\ndisc as it flies back to you. It's surprisingly cute.
BoundCp	If you're a fan of bouncy blobs of goo-like\nmaterial...you'll love these! For pulsating\nglobes of poison, they're oddly appealing.
Jab	A stripped-down ARM that's sacrificed aesthetics\nfor power and speed. It's basically only skin and\nbones now. Well, just bones. Poisonous bones.
Handlock	Cobbled together using spare parts from another\nARMS Labs creation, this baby breathes fire.\nIts developers think it's adorable. It's really not.
ParasolCp	A true DIY gem made out of an umbrella, some\ninfrared sensors, and an outdated electrode.\nLow cost, but highly effective.
NunchuckCp	It's a nunchuk that freezes its surroundings with a\ncyclone of chilly wind! Use it during a jump attack\nto see something really cool... Aren't you curious?
